GT: -c0*sqrt(A) - c1*A*exp(-c2*_s*t) + c3*_t*sin(log(A + c4))
Candidate formulas: 50

I need to analyze the Ground Truth (GT) expression and determine if any candidate can match it.

**GT numerical expression:**
`-0.12072*sqrt(A) - 0.12072*A*exp(-0.06862*t) + 0.85374*sin(log(A + 1))`

This has three terms:
1. `-0.12072*sqrt(A)` — a square root term in A
2. `-0.12072*A*exp(-0.06862*t)` — A times a decaying exponential in t
3. `0.85374*sin(log(A + 1))` — sine of log(A+1)

Let me search for candidates that could produce these three functional forms.

The key challenge is the `sin(log(A + 1))` term. Very few candidates have a `sin` function or `log` function that could produce this.

**Candidate 3:** `A*c0/(A + c1)**2 + c2 + c3*exp(A**c4*c5) + c6*log(A*c7*exp(c8*t) + 1)`
- Has `log(A*c7*exp(c8*t) + 1)` but not `sin(log(...))`. No match.

**Candidate 6:** `A*c0/(A + c1)**2 + c2 + c3*exp(A**c4*c5) + c6*exp(c7*t)*sin(c8*t + c9)`
- Has `sin` but only of `t`, not of `log(A+1)`. No match.

**Candidate 47:** `A*c0/(A + c1)**2 + c2 + c3*exp(A**2*c4) + c5*exp(c6*t)*sin(A*c7 + c8)`
- Has `sin(A*c7 + c8)` — sin of a linear function of A, not sin(log(A+1)). No match.

**Candidate 45:** `A*c0/(A + c1)**2 + A**c2*c3*exp(c4*t) + c5*exp(A*c6) + c7*t*exp(c8*t) + c9`
- Setting c2=1 gives `A*c3*exp(c4*t)` which matches the second GT term. But no sin(log(A+1)) term. No match.

**Candidate 46:** `A*A**c0*c1 + A*c2/(A + c3)**2 + A**c0*c4 + c5*t*exp(c6*t) + c7 + c8*exp(c9*t)`
- `A*A**c0 = A**(1+c0)`, setting c0=-0.5 gives `A**0.5 = sqrt(A)`. And `A**c0*c4 = A**(-0.5)*c4`. But still no sin(log(A+1)). No match.

Looking through all candidates systematically, none contain `sin(log(...))` or any composition that could yield `sin(log(A + 1))`.

Could `sin(log(A+1))` be approximated by some other functional form exactly? No — `sin(log(A+1))` is a transcendental function with specific oscillatory behavior in A that cannot be replicated by rational functions, exponentials, powers, or simple logarithms.

The only candidates with `sin` are #6 (sin of t) and #47 (sin of linear A). Neither can produce `sin(log(A+1))`.

Could any `exp(A**c*c)` term produce `sin(log(A+1))`? No — exponentials of powers of A are monotonic in A and cannot produce oscillatory behavior.

Could `log(A*c + 1)` terms match? `sin(log(A+1))` ≠ `c*log(A*c+1)` for any constants.

None of the candidates contain the functional form `sin(log(A + constant))`, and this cannot be algebraically constructed from the building blocks available in any of the candidates.

- `sqrt(A)` or `A^0.5`: None of the candidates have this explicitly, but some have `A^c` terms (like `A**c2` or `A**c0`) which could be set to 0.5.

Since `sin(log(A+1))` is a fundamentally different basis function from anything available in the candidates (polynomials, rational functions, exponentials, simple logs, simple sines), and by the principle of linear independence of basis functions, no combination of the available terms can exactly reproduce `sin(log(A+1))`.

The function `sin(log(A+1))` oscillates (albeit slowly for large A) and has a very specific non-monotonic behavior that cannot be replicated by:
- Rational functions of A
- `exp(A*c)` terms
- `log(A*c + 1)` terms
- `A^c` power terms
- Simple `sin(linear in A or t)` terms

None of the candidates contain `sin(log(...))`, and this function cannot be decomposed into any of the basis functions present in the candidates.

Let me verify candidates with `sin` more carefully:

- **Candidate 47**: `sin(A*c7 + c8)` - this is sin of a linear function of A, not of log(A+1)

Neither can match `sin(log(A+1))`.

Therefore, **no candidate can match the GT**.
